@2124

KHUL KHONGS MTSO SNA RDZONG GI SA CHA ZHIG STE, DUS RABS BCU
BDUN PAR BOD SA GNAS SRID GZHUNG GIS SA KHUL DE DBANG SGYUR
BYED 'GO TSUGS, DE KHUL SNGAR T'A LA'I BLA MA SKU PHRENG DRUG
PA TSANGS DBYANGS RGYA MTSO 'KHRUNGS YUL AO RGYAN GLING ZHES
GRAGS PA DE YANG YUL DER YOD,...

MON YUL GYI TSO LDING SUM CU SO GNYIS, SNGAR BOD SA GNAS SRID
GZHUNG SKABS, MTSO SNA RDZONG KHONGS MON YUL GYI TSO'AM LDING
STE, LEGS PO TSO BZHI, SPANG CHEN LDING DRUG DVAGS PA TSO
BRGYAD, LA 'OG YUL GSUM, SBRANG NANG TSO DRUG RONG NANG TSO
BZHI, SHA 'UG HRO BYANG DVAGS BCAS SO GNYIS,...
